              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8310179-blacky-romance-addict?shelf=read-paranormal">read-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8310179-blacky-romance-addict?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8310179-blacky-romance-addict?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8310179-blacky-romance-addict?shelf=read-2013">read-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8310179-blacky-romance-addict?shelf=5-stars-for-enjoyment">5-stars-for-enjoyment</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8310179-blacky-romance-addict?shelf=favorite-paranormal">favorite-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8310179-blacky-romance-addict?shelf=read-2012">read-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer341772913" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10156001423961040354"><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736047.jpg' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"He waited for his conscience to start screaming.<br/>He prepared himself for an overwhelming desolation that he had been with another female.<br/>He was… ready for something, anything to cough up out of his chest—despair, anger, frustration.<br/>All he got was the sense that what had just happened was the beginning, not an end."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/><b><br/>Lover Reborn is a heartbreaking story, even though it has a happy end.<br/>Watching Tohrment and his suffering, trying to let go of Wellsie... It was sad and beautiful at the sa</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10156001423961040354" style="display:none"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736047.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"He waited for his conscience to start screaming.<br>He prepared himself for an overwhelming desolation that he had been with another female.<br>He was… ready for something, anything to cough up out of his chest—despair, anger, frustration.<br>All he got was the sense that what had just happened was the beginning, not an end."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b><br>Lover Reborn is a heartbreaking story, even though it has a happy end.<br>Watching Tohrment and his suffering, trying to let go of Wellsie... It was sad and beautiful at the same time, because of what he found with No'One. <br>It was a slow romance, full of sadness, but I loved it all the same.<br>This one definitely goes to one of my favorites from this series! </b><br><br><br><br><br><b>The story</b><br><br><br>The only thing keeping Tohr alive is his obsession with avenging his wife's murder. He is focused only on killing lessers, and is getting weaker and weaker as the days go by, because he's stopped eating and feeding.<br>Lassiter is the only one that can get to Tohr, and he's doing whatever he can to help him, because he's here on a mission to free Wellsie from the In Between.<br>After seeing how Tohr reacts to No'One, he gets a brilliant idea to get those two together :D<br>It works, in a way, but at the cost of both Tohr's and No'One's feelings.<br>They will have to get over their pasts, and make a new future for themselves...<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I don’t want to hurt you,” he said, feeling like he wanted to return the favor.<br>“You won’t. I know you are still in love with your mate, and I do not blame you. What you had with her is a once-in-a-lifetime love.”<br>“What about you?”<br>“I have no need or desire to take her place. And I accept you just as you are, in any fashion you choose to come to me. Or not, if that is the way it must be.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><b>The story</b> - The previous book was pretty much insta-love, and this one is as far from insta-love as you can get.<br>Very slow in the romance part, and I prefer it that way, otherwise it wouldn't be believable. It took Tohr a lot of time to find himself again, and that's great, as I said, totally believable :)<br>This book is really about letting go of the loved ones, and moving on with life, and it was done wonderfully, it was difficult and heartbreaking, so very sad, but beautiful in the end.<br>There was some action here, but not much. A couple of intense scenes, especially the ambush one.<br><br><br><b>The characters<br><br>*will be spoilerish!!!!!*<br><br>Lassiter</b> - He has a big role in this one (yay!!!), an angel sent to Earth to redeem himself, he has to free Wellsie from the In Between, and for that, he has to make Tohr move on with his life and let her go.<br>Of course, that isn't as easy as it sounds, because Tohr's suffering is too great, he loved her too much to let her go.<br>Lassiter doesn't really do compassion, he doesn't care about anyone, but he forms a friendship with Tohr, and by the end of it, he's willing to do whatever it takes to see Tohr and No'One have a happy end.<br>What he did at the end of the book! &lt;3 I knew I loved him for a reason &lt;3 And I can't wait for him to get his own book, I just know that it's going to be amazing &lt;3<br><br><b>Xhex/John</b> - They go through a tough time here, mostly because they didn't know what they got into when they got mated, and it takes more than just being in love to make a life with someone.<br>John is overprotective of Xhex, and after she gets hurt, he basically forbids her to go out in the field.<br>Well, I don't have to say anything more about how that turned out :DD<br>Xhex is a trained killer, she can hold her own, but the Brotherhood stands by John on this one, so she leaves the mansion and goes back to her previous line of work with Trez.<br>It was really hard to see them unhappy, and I seriously didn't know how it could get better, but I'm glad how it all worked out, and how John realised he has to change his thinking when it comes to Xhex and her fighting with the Brotherhood.<br><br><b>The Band of Bastards</b> - I still don't like them. They are just totally boring to me and I'd rather skip all the scenes with them -.-<br>BUT ok, what happened with them:<br>We learn some more about Throe, why exactly did he join the Bastards, and he falls in love in this book. Whatever. <br>Xcor is making some devious plans on overtaking the throne and killing Wrath. He too falls in love in this book. Whatever.<br>They have and orgy that I just didn't find sexy to read AT ALL. In fact, I don't think I liked any of the sex scenes from them since they first showed up. No thank you for me. Big no thank you.<br><br><b>Assail</b> - He's the new vampire drug lord. Have no idea if he'll be good or bad, but he's interesting. Doesn't get on my nerves at all and I actually wanted to read scenes with him (good sign!!!)<br><br><b>Layla</b> - Well, she falls in love in this book too. I'd like to care, but I really don't. I shudder to think how I'll get through her book when the time comes. I hope there will be a LOT of side characters. A LOT!!! In fact, I could do with a novella. A very short one. Why torture us with a whole book?? Especially since the main guy is gonna be <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Xcor (pukes). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>Qhuinn/Blay</b> - Not many scenes here but there were a few touching ones, when Qhuinn was hurt in the hospital &lt;3 and that ending!!!<br>"Our future has come."<br>&lt;3 Finally!!!!! It took a lot of time for Qhuinn to figure things out, and I'm glad he did it here :)<br>There was a complication with Layla, that drove Qhuay apart even more. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She went in her needing and Qhuinn serviced her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Don't know how that's going to play out :SSSSS<br><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736048.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"He must never know, she thought as she closed her eyes and rested her head on his chest.<br>He must never, ever know what beat within her heart for him.<br>It would ruin everything."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>No'One has a long history with Tohrment and Darius, a few centuries ago, they saved her from a sympath who raped her and left her pregnant.<br>After she delivered the baby, she took Tohr's dagger and killed herself. That's how she ended up in the Sanctuary, looking after the Chosen, and redeeming herself in being a servant.<br>After coming down to the Brotherhood's mansion, she still continues to be a servant, even though it bothers everyone.<br>She feels she owes a debt to Tohr and wants to repay him, so with Lassiter's little push, she agrees to feed him and make him strong again.<br>That leads to both of them getting closer, and No'One falling in love, even though she knows it will never be requited.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"His fingers running lightly over her skin were intoxicating, drawing her closer to this flame that she could not see. Closing her eyes, she allowed herself to fly far away from any worries or preoccupations, until she knew nothing but the sensations in her body.<br>Indeed, as she fed him, she was fed herself, a part of her innermost soul nourished for the first time."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>As mush as this book might be about Tohr getting over Wellsie, it's about No'One as well, her finally breaking free of her self-punishment, and embracing life with all the good things it brings.<br>Bit by bit we see her changing, from the totally hooded, robed person, to her becoming Autumn, free to show herself, and enjoying life, and being with Tohr.<br>I liked her very much, and most of the time I felt sorry for her cause Tohr acted like a jerk to her :((((<br>She knew he still loved Wellsie, but she wanted to help him get better, and be with him in any way she could.<br>When Xhex took her in, that scene was great, I was glad to see them getting closer.<br>After <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[her needing <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, that was BRUTAL. My heart went out to her and I couldn't believe Thor acted that way.<br>The ending, when everything was revealed, it was terrible! Just terrible :(( I felt bad for both of them :(<br>But I'm glad it still ended up a HEA &lt;3 They both deserve it!<br><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380805013i/3123817.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You’re beautiful. Every inch of you. Don’t think for a moment there’s anything wrong with you. We clear?”<br>“But—”<br>“Nope. I’m not hearing that.” Bending down, he pressed his lips to her shin, her calf, her ankle, tracing the scars, caressing them. “Beautiful. All of you.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>Having lost his wife and unborn child at the beginning of the series, Tohr has gone through a lot, and has lost the will to live, but unwilling to commit suicide because that would mean he couldn't be with his Wellsie when he dies.<br>He is focused only on fighting and avenging his dead, and soon it takes his tool on his body, because he hasn't fed from anyone in a long time.<br>When No'One offers, he knows it's safe, because she could never feel anything for him, nor he for her.<br>As time goes on, they start to have a relationship, mostly because Tohr thinks he has to do it to let Wellsie go. <br>Eventually he fears he's betraying his wife for being with another woman, and he can't deal with having any feelings for No'One.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Autumn is my favorite season of the year,” he said after a time. “It’s not that I’m chicking out or anything… but I like the leaves when they turn red and orange. They’re beautiful in the moonlight, but more to the point, it’s an impossible transformation. The green of spring and summer is just a shadow of the trees’ true identity, and all that color as the nights grow cold is a miracle every stinking time it happens. It’s like they’re making up for the loss of the warmth with all their fire. I like… Autumn.” He stared into her eyes. “You’re like that. You’re beautiful and you burn brightly—and it’s time for you to come out. So I say… Autumn.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>First, it was heartbreaking seeing Tohr mourning his wife. So, so difficult to read :((( <br>I can't begin to understand what it must be like, and I'm glad this book didn't make it a piece of cake for Tohr to get over it. I took months and months of them going from zero, to being in love at the end of the book. Nothing was easy for them in any part of the book, and it made me love them even more... <br>So I am very happy with how it all turned out.<br><br>Second, Tohr's behavior toward No'One was pretty much terrible. He was a total jerk in a lot of situations, I couldn't believe it, but there it was. <br>The pool scene when he sees her floating. OMG, could he have been more of a jerk??? I think not! I wanted to kick him in the head!!!<br>The first feeding was awful. Just terrible, poor No'One.<br>The sex between them... I liked that, Tohr was nice about it, knowing what she went through, but after a time it got terrible too because he kept shutting her out of his life, feeling like he would cheat on Wellsie if he had sex with No'One.<br>The second pool scene &lt;3 now that was just wonderful &lt;3<br>The <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[needing <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>... Shoot me now. No, shoot Tohr now! What a moron! I couldn't believe what he did, and then later, what he said to her :((((<br>He is just lucky she forgave him, very damn lucky!<br>But even with all the jerkish things he did, that ending was so heartbreaking, I couldn't not forgive him!<br>I cried like a baby :((((<br>To have him suffer so much :((((((((((<br>Terrible. Just terrible :(<br>So yes, they both definitely deserved a HEA, and I'm glad they got it! <br><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>My favorite quotes from other characters:</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736049.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736050.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“This is not about safety—it’s about control.”<br>Bullshit! You were hurt less than twenty-four hours ago—<br>“Fine. I have an idea. I want to keep you safe—so how about you stop fighting.” She glared over her shoulder at Wrath. “You gonna back me up, my lord? How about the rest of you fools? Let’s put the skirt and the panty hose on John, shall we? Come on, back my ass up. No? You don’t think that would be ‘fair’?”<br>John’s temper flared, and he just… He didn’t mean to do what he did. It just happened.<br>He stomped his boot, creating a thunderous noise, and pointed… directly at Tohr.<br><br>Awkward. Horrid. Silence.<br><br>---------------------------------------------<br><br>I’m giving you your space, but know this: I WILL wait forever for you.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736051.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736052.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>With a groan, he shoved his palms into the shimmering silver pool of blood beneath him, and flopped over like the side of beef he was.<br>“Wow,” she breathed.<br>“I know, right? Hung like a horse.”<br>“If you’re really nice—and you live through this—I’ll promise not to tell V.”<br>“About my size.”<br>She laughed a little. “No, that you assumed I’d look at you in any fashion other than professionally.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736052.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’m just trying to get through to you.” Lassiter sat down, cracked open a beer, and looked tired. “Man, this angel crap… it’s so fucking hard to influence anything. I’ve never had a problem with free will before, but for shit’s sake, I wish I could just I Dream of Jeannie you to where you need to be.”<br>--------------------------------<br>"This… display… across the way? Not sure, not fine, not dandy.<br>That kind of suffering was a canyon, a purgatory of its own for someone who had not died. And damned if the angel had any clue how to drag the Brother out of it.<br>Frankly, he was having enough trouble just playing witness."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736053.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"And then the king put the hand that bore the black diamond ring of the race to his own chest, right in the middle, directly over his heart… and slowly, gingerly, with the help of his shellan, bent over at the waist.<br>To bow at Qhuinn.<br>As all the blood drained out of Qhuinn’s head, and he wondered what the fuck the most important vampire on the planet was doing, someone started clapping slowly.<br>Clap. Clap. Clap!<br>Others joined in, until the entire assembly, from Phury and Cormia, to Z and Bella and baby Nalla, to Fritz and his staff… to Vishous and Payne and their mates, to Butch and Marissa and Rehv and Ehlena… were clapping for him with tears unshed in their eyes."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736054.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379705i/736053.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Blay didn’t look away.<br>And for the first time… neither did Qhuinn.<br>He didn’t know whether the emotion was about his cousin—it probably was—but he’d take it: He stared right back at Blaylock and let everything he had in his heart show in his face.<br>He just let that shit fly."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><b>My future has come, at last!</b><br><br><br><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_181949536" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/181949536" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/181949536?book_show_action=true">Jul 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13101894-lover-reborn">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of the series</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2012_reads">2012_reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=jr-ward-jessica-bird">jr-ward-jessica-bird</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer181949536" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12002163592833386395"><i>(*big satisfied sigh*)</i><br/>Well, I <i>was</i> a little worried about how this book (Tohr's story) might play out. Tohr has been in misery over losing his Wellsie for just over 15 months (has it only been 15 months? It seems so much longer...) Anyway, in this book he has to move on and get past his grief because Wellsie is <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ stuck in the "In Between"--a kind of purgatory, and she's not in "The Fade", the happy place where vampires go when they die. If Tohr doesn't snap to it, Wellsie and their </span></span>
  <span id="freeText12002163592833386395" style="display:none"><i>(*big satisfied sigh*)</i><br>Well, I <i>was</i> a little worried about how this book (Tohr's story) might play out. Tohr has been in misery over losing his Wellsie for just over 15 months (has it only been 15 months? It seems so much longer...) Anyway, in this book he has to move on and get past his grief because Wellsie is <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ stuck in the "In Between"--a kind of purgatory, and she's not in "The Fade", the happy place where vampires go when they die. If Tohr doesn't snap to it, Wellsie and their unborn son wiill cease to exist--no Fade for them. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>So that's the main plot going on in <b>Lover Reborn</b>. Tohr reconnects with a woman from his past (before Wellsie)--No 'One. No'One is actually Xhex's mother (I think her past was told in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7046495.Lover_Mine__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___8_" title="Lover Mine (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #8) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Mine</a>). Tohr is attracted to the pretty, petite blonde No'One but of course doesn't want to be--that would be a betrayal to his beloved Wellsie and he just can't see himself loving another woman after Wellsie. But...the angel Lassiter lets Tohr in on what's happening to Wellsie, how she's <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ not in the Fade and is wasting away in the "In Between", <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and Tohr is appropriately horrified. If Tohr "physically" moves on with another woman, will that be enough to save his beloved?<br><br><i>Tohr</i>...<br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=13364_179165372860_632437860_291875-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380352580i/705996.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I think like most BDB fans, I couldn't imagine Tohr with anyone else. I loved Tohr and Wellsie! I mean, it was such a shock when Wellsie was killed off, I grieved along with Tohr. But Tohr really took his grief to the next level...I mean he <i>grieved</i>! And I hated seeing him that lost and miserable, so I was ready to see how J.R. Ward was going to move him forward. And let me tell you, it wasn't easy, but it was oh so satisfying! I loved every minute of it--the reluctance, the angst, the giving in, the passion, the denial of feelings, the cruel truth, and the acceptance...all the stages of grief that he went through. It wasn't about finding a new love to replace Wellsie in his heart, but finding the courage to accept what was and move forward. I just thought the whole plot was beautifully conceived and written.<br><br><i>No'One/Autumn</i>...<br><a href="http://s880.photobucket.com/albums/ac3/aunteecr/?action=view&amp;current=nooneautumn.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380352580i/705997.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really liked No'One, or Autumn, as she came to be known (after Tohr renamed her in one of the most moving parts of the book). She had her own journey to go through right along with Tohr, had some truths to face about herself too, and it was definitely not all smooth sailing. I thought her love scenes with Tohr were smokin' <i>hot</i> (can Ward write erotica or what?), and wow, the effect her 'needing' had on some other couples...<i>whew</i>!<br><br>Well, besides Tohr and No'One, this book had plenty to offer:<br><br>*Xhex and John Matthew are having trouble in their marriage. John Matthew doesn't know if he can stand to have Xhex fighting along with the Brothers--what if she gets hurt and he ends up like Tohr? Can they come to some kind of compromise or is their marriage doomed?<br>I love JM...that's all I'm going to say about this. *sigh*<br><br>*The Band of Bastards (led by the cruel and powerful Xcor) are working at dethroning Wrath. Will they be successful?<br>I'm rather enjoying this storyline. I like how we're finding out more and more about Xcor and what makes him tick, and oh boy, if he ever does connect with <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Layla <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, look out!<br><br>*Lassiter! He's desperate to help Tohr, at first to help himself get out of the trouble he's in with the Maker, but later...he really does want to help Tohr and No'One<br>I loved this quirky, TV-lovin' angel! He's so funny, he's got some <i>great</i> lines in the story...every time he showed up the pages came alive. I hope he gets a story soon because I want to find out more about him!<br><br>*Qhuinn and Layla. Ooooh, they do something that could have far reaching consequences. Oh yeah. Hmmn...can't <i>wait</i> to see what happens there...<br><br>*Qhuinn and Blay. Yesss, get away from Saxton! Sadly, not much happens with them in this book, but... Oh yeah, this is going to heat up soon...<br><br>*Cameos from all the Brothers and a few of the shellans. I just love when the Brothers pop in and out of the book. I love seeing them, even if they only have a few words to say. I especially loved the touching scene at the end where each of the Brothers presented Tohr <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ with gifts to get him through Wellsie's Fade ceremony. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> What a scene that was. Brought tears to my eyes. I love these guys.<br><br>So yes, Ward left us with some unfinished business, which is fine with me. She wrapped up the main storyline but left us with just enough to keep us hanging and eagerly anticipating the next installment, as we should be. You know, I've never been disappointed with any of the BDB books. Of course I have my favorites, but each story manages to move the series along in the direction Ms. Ward wants to go, and I'm happy to give her free reign and to follow along. <b>Lover Reborn</b> was an immensely satisfying, steamy read, and did right by Tohr. Ward is such a skilled storyteller that I'm eager to immerse myself in her colorful world. Now, when's the next one due out? 5 stars</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="12002163592833386395" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_158777846" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/158777846" />
    <a title="Buggy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3099666-buggy"><img alt="Buggy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1289702969p2/3099666.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/158777846?book_show_action=true">Apr 04, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Buggy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Buggy" href="/user/show/3099666-buggy">Buggy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer158777846" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8216618021819464695">*<b>SPOILER FREE*</b><br/>Opening Line <i>"The bastard's taking the bridge! He's mine!"</i><br/><br/>Wow, I honestly don’t know where to begin with this review. To say that this was good is an understatement. To say that it knocked me on my ass and left me a drained, emotional wreck, is far closer to the truth. Yup, LOVER REBORN did me in, talk about your gauntlet of emotions, I mean I expected some angst but jeez! I cried (I mean really cried) I laughed, I sighed, I swore, I groaned and I gasped but in the end I also smile</span>
  <span id="freeText8216618021819464695" style="display:none">*<b>SPOILER FREE*</b><br />Opening Line <i>"The bastard's taking the bridge! He's mine!"</i><br /><br />Wow, I honestly don’t know where to begin with this review. To say that this was good is an understatement. To say that it knocked me on my ass and left me a drained, emotional wreck, is far closer to the truth. Yup, LOVER REBORN did me in, talk about your gauntlet of emotions, I mean I expected some angst but jeez! I cried (I mean really cried) I laughed, I sighed, I swore, I groaned and I gasped but in the end I also smiled. <br /><br />As much as I was anticipating this book it was also with a heavy dose of apprehension; was I ready to see Tohrment find love again? Was he ready? Were any of us really ready to let Wellsie go? And most importantly could Ward make me believe in this new love? The answer is a resounding yes, I think in part because it doesn’t happen quickly (or easily) Reborn has been broken into 4 sections (1 per season) so that this book takes place over the period of a year. And it was over that year and all the shit that goes down (and oh does the shit ever go down) that Ward made me believe. <br /><br />Starting where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8492319.Lover_Unleashed__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___9_" title="Lover Unleashed (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #9) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">Lover Unleashed</a> left off and with her usual flair Ward throws us into <b>“Spring”</b> and right into the action and pain that is Tohr. Chasing down a group of Lessers, Tohr is now relentless in his pursuit of the enemy, basically only drawing breathe to “ahvenge” his murdered wife and son. Tonight’s hunt sees Tohr launching himself off a bridge as John and Qhuinn watch helplessly from below, John issuing a silent scream as Tohr falls. And so it begins. Through 572 pages Ward proceeds to give us everything we want and then some…<br /><br />Without going into spoiler territory (which is going to be hard) I can tell you of course that this is Tohr and No’one’s story. These two have a long history together and are both equally broken so it makes sense for them to get together. Lassiter is helping to move them along on the love train (in his own way) and as it turns out with a sense of urgency. John and Xhex also play key roles in their story, giving us some absolutely filthy-hot love scenes as well as showing us a marriage in transition. <br /><br />Xcor and his Band Of Bastards are back and gaining strength in Caldwell. They do things here that… can never be forgiven. Sending one Brother on a mission under a decree of death. New and mysterious characters are introduced (Assail) while others are fleshed out (Throe and Zyphor.) We’re still all mixed up in the whole hot-mess that is Layla/Qhinn/Blay/Saxton; however that’s all about to change:) The Blind King still kicks ass, Ward throws a “needing” (or two) our way and gives us details of a ceremony that absolutely broke my heart. We also bare witness to a battle that gave me heart palpitations for all of its 60 pages and left some Brothers with life threatening injuries. <br /><br />Somehow through all this Ward also manages to give us time with each and every member of the Brotherhood mansion. We get to see everyone doing their thing, giving us some special moment with each of them and that in itself says something because there are so many characters now. There also aren’t any “lesser” POV’s to suffer through; we don’t travel back to the old country or to the other side to hang with the chosen (verily.) And I have to compliment Ward on toning down the product placement and Wardisms. This book just flowed beautifully.<br /><br />In fact I would have to say that Ward has hit her pinnacle with Lover Reborn. The balance here is just right; the romance, the action, the surprises and the healing. I honestly never knew where this was going to go and when that happens you’re guaranteed a great ride. <br /><br />And now for the good news Blay and Qhuinn have been officially announced as book #11! That’s right the wait is over. It looks like Ward has worked a miracle with her publisher because their story was originally to be a novella and now they’re getting their very own Hardcover instalment. Way to go boys. See you Spring 2013<br /><br />"Thats right, buddy.<i> Our future has come.</i> <br /><br />287jb5+</span>
  <a data-text-id="8216618021819464695" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/168923134" />
    <a title="Camilla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4072455-camilla"><img alt="Camilla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554065817p2/4072455.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/168923134?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Camilla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Camilla" href="/user/show/4072455-camilla">Camilla</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13101894-lover-reborn">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4072455-camilla?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4072455-camilla?shelf=read-and-sent-to-j">read-and-sent-to-j</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer168923134&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer168923134" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15797040966872836177"><i>May 17th 2011</i><br/><br/>Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! <br/><br/>Tohr who? ;oP<br/><br/>------------------------------<br/><i>March 27th (finished at 01.30 in the morning, so technically it's the 28th I guess)</i><br/><br/>Done.. And I dont know what to say really. I should be happy, I should be freaking out, crazy excited, all over the place, considering that last Qhuay scene.. But I'm not.. I'm <i>so</i> fucking not happy right now..<br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[I may be the most evil person, but I do <b>not</b> want Qhuinn as Layla's babydad</span></span>
  <span id="freeText15797040966872836177" style="display:none"><i>May 17th 2011</i><br /><br />Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! Qhuay! <br /><br />Tohr who? ;oP<br /><br />------------------------------<br /><i>March 27th (finished at 01.30 in the morning, so technically it's the 28th I guess)</i><br /><br />Done.. And I dont know what to say really. I should be happy, I should be freaking out, crazy excited, all over the place, considering that last Qhuay scene.. But I'm not.. I'm <i>so</i> fucking not happy right now..<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I may be the most evil person, but I do <b>not</b> want Qhuinn as Layla's babydaddy. Not even if she somehow died and the kid got raised by Qhuinn and Blay..<br /><br />I do NOT want this baby..<br /><br />The thing is.. Everything in this book points to a child, and if that happens..? <br /><br />No.. just... No..<br /><br />Ugghh!!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Actual review tomorrow.. <br /><br />------------------------------------------<br /><i>March 28th</i> <br /><br />At work the next day, trying to write my actual review..<br /><br />So what did I think..<br /><br />I’m trying really hard to <i>not</i> think about the things I didn’t like, cause with as little sleep as I got last night, and the fact that I still feel exhausted, I’m pretty sure I would start bawling my eyes out, and that’s not the best thing to do at work.. Well.. At least that’s what I’ve been told..<br /><br />I think I should just focus on the things I <i>did</i> like, and then let out all my Qhuayla frustration elsewhere..<br /><br />I did, in fact, really like No’One.. And holy fuck, that was a big ass surprise for me. The only thing I’ve been waiting for with this book was the Qhuay parts, and I honestly haven’t even given No’One a thought the last year.. So it surprised the hell out of me when she actually made me tear up.. more than once..<br /><br />This is Tohr’s second love story if you will. He had Wellsie, and this book sees him through a year of his life where he once again comes face to face with No’One, who he once met, and lived with for a year in a cave, while she was preggers. Sadly, she (No’One) had been kidnapped and raped, so after she gave birth to the little girl (who we all know now, was Xhex) she killed herself with Tohr’s black dagger. This happened a long time ago, long before Tohr was mated off to Wellsie. <br /><br />In this book we find out that Wellsie is stuck in the <i>In Between</i> and to “save” her and their babyboy, Tohr has to let her go and move on. In the land of the BDB “<i>moving on</i>” and “<i>letting go</i>” of your dead mate is apparently fucking someone else… Ok… <i>So</i> not commenting on that one… *rolls eyes*<br /><br />Anywho.. So yeah, I really, really liked <s>Autumn</s> No’One and her storyline. With Tohr and with Xhex too. I was surprised at how tough she was and how she could talk back to Tohr when he was being an ass, because holy flipping hell, Tohr acted like an ass! I mean, if I had the opportunity to bitch-slap one person in that book, I almost want to pick Tohr over Layla..<br /><br />Umm.. Ok, no… I want to bitch-slap Layla… Pretty please?!<br /><br />For the life of me I cannot fathom how JRW can make Qhuinn have sex with Layla..<br /><br />She KNOWS that his HEA is someone else, another guy for fucks sake.. Why, <b>WHY</b> does he have to sleep with Layla? Put some fucking drugs in her and help her with her needing, don’t put your fucking c*ck in her, you stupid SOB!! Arghhh…<br /><br /><i>Pheewww</i><br /><br />The thing that bothers me the most is the; Why? Why do they need to do this? There is no freaking point to the storyline, <i>if</i> of course, JRW <i>doesn’t</i> plan to bring a Qhuayla baby in to the world.. And after reading this book, I’m actually kinda scared, that <i>that</i> is exactly her plan.. Why else have them screw each other? There is no freaking point!!<br /><br />Am I too invested in Qhuinn and Blay? Maybe.. Probably.. But I can’t help what I feel. And I feel very, <i>very</i> strongly about these 2 boys, and if she does this.. If she makes Qhuinn be a father to Layla’s baby, she’s fucking up Qhuinn’s story.. and <i>that</i> I will never forgive..<br /><br />Over all, I liked this book.. I couldn’t give it any stars last night when I finished it, ‘cause I was too exhausted from crying too much, and too numb from worrying about the 2 people I love the most in this series. <br /><br />After some thought, I think I’ll give it 4 stars. Qhuinn, Layla, and Tohr being a bitch, makes me want to take 1 away, but then I think of No’One and how she made me tear up, and then I’m ok with 4 stars.. <br /></span>

<div id="review_884887838" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/884887838" />
    <a title="P " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25327841-p"><img alt="P " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489853536p2/25327841.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/884887838?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P " class="user" itemprop="url" name="P " href="/user/show/25327841-p">P </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer884887838" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8491856132875380908"><b>
  <blockquote>“Life was short, no matter how many days you were granted. And people were precious, each and every one, no matter how many you were lucky enough to have in your life. And love... love was worth dying for.<br/>Worth living for, too.” </blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479721151i/21225853._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book is tragic. Tohr has to move on and leave his past behind if he want his shellin to rest in peace, it's not easy when she is the only thing he can hold on to even he passed the storms, it still hurts like hell for him. I didn't expected too much about this b</span>
  <span id="freeText8491856132875380908" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>“Life was short, no matter how many days you were granted. And people were precious, each and every one, no matter how many you were lucky enough to have in your life. And love... love was worth dying for.<br>Worth living for, too.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479721151i/21225853._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book is tragic. Tohr has to move on and leave his past behind if he want his shellin to rest in peace, it's not easy when she is the only thing he can hold on to even he passed the storms, it still hurts like hell for him. I didn't expected too much about this book. The story was not my cuppa, yet it was engaging and sad at the same time. I loved No'One, her personality was precarious because what she has been through is unbearable for me.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Aha!" Lassiter pointed at the boob tube. "You motherfucker! I knew you were the father!” </blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479721151i/21225854._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lover Reborn has the different vibes from the other books, this book consists of joy, sadness, pain and hope. I almost cried for Tohr and No'One; they loses in their own ways and wants to fight for someone they love. The book itself is capable of wrenching my gut, but actually I don't like when Tohr and No'One choose to avoid each other, it frustrated me so much.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Life’s meant to be lived blind—that’s how you don’t take shit for granted.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>All in all, this book is a real page-turner. Every detail made me interested and wanted to continue until the last page. I hated and loved Tohr. I want to hold him close and tell him that everything is okay, at least for now.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479721151i/21225855._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="570" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/zz6ACQ">https://goo.gl/zz6ACQ</a></span>

<div id="review_172499461" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/172499461" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/172499461?book_show_action=true">May 31, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">PNR/UFR fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=brotherhood">brotherhood</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-to-die-for">hero-to-die-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorite-or-autobuy-author">favorite-or-autobuy-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=all-things-spring-challenge">all-things-spring-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=widower">widower</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=celibate-or-less-experienced-hero">celibate-or-less-experienced-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer172499461&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer172499461" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4660317309833471312"><b>***Bigtime Spoiler Warning. I can’t write this review without them. Sorry!<br/>****Super-duper Long Review Disclaimer! I have so much to say!</b><br/><br/>When I started reading this series back around 2005 or 2006, I was drawn into the dark, seductive, dangerous world of JR Ward’s vampires, and something took root in me. I knew I would come back for more when I finished Dark Lover, and so I did. Again and again. Every year, I look forward to a new book in this series, and rightfully so. I believed the culmination</span>
  <span id="freeText4660317309833471312" style="display:none"><b>***Bigtime Spoiler Warning. I can’t write this review without them. Sorry!<br />****Super-duper Long Review Disclaimer! I have so much to say!</b><br /><br />When I started reading this series back around 2005 or 2006, I was drawn into the dark, seductive, dangerous world of JR Ward’s vampires, and something took root in me. I knew I would come back for more when I finished Dark Lover, and so I did. Again and again. Every year, I look forward to a new book in this series, and rightfully so. I believed the culmination of my love for this series would be Lover Mine, since John Matthew and Xhex are two of my favorite characters. While that book will always have a special place in my heart, I am happy to say that I still believe this series has more to offer me with every book. <br /><br />I knew I would enjoy Lover Reborn, but I had some anxieties about it because it’s a pivotal entry, and a difficult storyline to read about (and to write about, from Ward’s perspective). So many expectations! I am happy to say I believe that Ward has stayed true to who she is as a writer with this book.<br /><br />Tohrment always seemed like the most grounded, stable, mature member of the Brotherhood. When this series began, he was a family man, happily mated to Wellesandra. He was the voice of reason in the Brotherhood, and many looked to him for advice, leadership, and moderation. All that disappeared in a single act of violence, one that tore his beloved shellan and their unborn son away from Tohr, leaving a broken wreck of a male behind.<br /><br />The opinions are varied. Many feel that it was too soon for Tohr to find another mate. Some believe he never should be mated again. Some want Wellsie to come back. As much as I love Wellsie, the realist in me didn’t expect her to be brought back. I feel that this would be way too fairy tale a resolution for this quite dark series. Personally, I would rather someone who had lost their wife/husband to move on and find love again. If I died, I would want my husband to be happy in this life. I believe Wellsie definitely felt the same way. Although I’m not a widow and I haven’t lost my soulmate, I have lost people that I loved, and grief is a part of life. It hurts like nothing else, and the loss makes a void in one’s life that cannot easily (nor should it be) be filled with anything else. Yet, over time, you feel those horrible claws of loss easing their way out of your soul and psyche, and you feel the healing begin. I for one feel that Ms. Ward did a very good job at portraying this with Tohr’s journey in this book.<br /><br />There is no question whatsoever that Tohr loved Wellsie. But I loved the message that part of loving her was letting her go, and allowing her to go to her eternal resting place, and moving on and living his life. It felt right to me how the storyline showed that Tohr was actually keeping Wellsie from going to the Fade by his horrible, wrenching, unchanging grief. Although this is fiction, I do believe in the message about healing from grief being so integral to the process. And that felt so real to me.<br /><br />My other concern was how Tohr and No’One’s relationship would develop. I didn’t want the whole book to be about how No’One would never measure up in his eyes, and that she was just a consolation prize, since Wellsie was gone. On the other hand, I didn’t want Wellsie to be forgotten about like being gone meant she didn’t matter anymore. That makes a very hard path to walk for a writer. For me, there was a lot of symmetry in how Tohr and No’One came together. It was naturalistic to the story, and I was satisfied with the outcome. Like most of the courtships in these books, there was a rocky road; but both Tohr and No’One both learn and grow from the experience. <br /><br /><b>No’One</b><br />Many readers have speculated on her, and how she could end up being Tohr’s mated shellan. In Lover Mine, I learned enough about her to think that there could be a foundation between her and Tohr. <br /><br />Although Tohr spent many years with Wellsie, and their love was the cornerstone of his life, he also had a very crucial relationship with No’One in his formative years. As a young vampire, he helped to save No’One when she was kidnapped and abused by a sympath male. He nursed and cared for her through her pregnancy, and he buried her when she killed herself, with his dagger. From a spiritual perspective, an unbreakable bond formed between them that is pivotal to the healing that is necessary for both. So it made sense for them to come together for me. She wasn’t just a random female that dropped out of nowhere. <br /><br /> Regardless, Tohr doesn’t make it easy for No’One to claim his heart. He is truly mean to her a couple of times in this book, and I wanted to slap him upside the head. And she hates herself so much, that she doesn’t feel she has the right to be loved. So No’One has to go through a sea change to claim her happiness in this world, this time around. It was painful to see how she hurt herself emotionally, how she denied her right to happiness, but that too was realistic. How often do we blame ourselves for the mistakes we make and the bad things that happen to us in this life, which aren’t our faults? We feel that we have to claim that misfortune and assume that we deserved it. No’One had an elephant’s weight of guilt sitting on her back, and until she divested herself of it, she could be no freer to love than Tohr was. There was balance in that. <br /><br /><b>Tohr and No’One</b><br />Tohr is a really good guy. Despite all the horrible grief he suffered, he still tried to be courteous and to make sure that No’One had what she needed, as far as he could give it. Other than his two freakouts, which were pretty nasty, I think he treated her well. He didn’t make any false promises. I loved how he gave her a new name that he felt was worthy of her because she refused to go by her name when she was a young member of the Glymera. Autumn is a very fitting name, and I loved it. I liked how it tied into the cover so well. And it also ties into the whole storyline. People think of Autumn as the harbinger to the darkest part of the year. Autumn is a time of transition. It has a beauty all its own. It’s the season when the bright beauty of summer edges into the crisp purity of winter. Autumn is like a time of rest for the earth. To me, that is representative of what Tohr is going through. He is learning to live without Wellsie and to find joy and beauty in what had promised to be a very dark future. <br /><br />The love scenes between Tohr and No’One/Autumn were very good. It showed that although Tohr’s first shellan had died, his heart didn’t have to die with her, nor his body and his capacity to feel desire for another woman. I liked that they eased into it over several months. I also liked how Autumn was able to see that she could have joy in a physical relationship with male. Being kidnapped and assaulted by the sympath male had made her feel disgust for males. With a gentle, loving male like Tohr, she was able to embrace the physical side of being a female. It felt right to me.<br /><br /><b>No’One and Xhex</b><br />I loved the bonding moments between No'One and Xhex. They were able to meet as adults and to see each other outside of the fact that Xhex was conceived in a horrible way for No’One, and she had given up Xhex. Xhex realized how much her mother valued and felt pride in her, even though she didn’t meet the Glymera’s standards for beauty and success for a woman. These bonding moments made me happy because Xhex didn’t have a lot of people in her life to open up with and feel acceptance from, and she was going through a rough time with JM and how the Brothers tended to have a sexist viewpoint of her abilities in the field. They could meet on equal ground as women in love, and be there for each other. Those parts warmed my heart. I’m glad they found each other again.<br /><br /><b>Tohr and John Matthew</b><br />Since Tohr views JM as his son, and vice versa, this was a crucial part of the novel to see them come together again. JM was able to help Tohr with his grief, and Tohr was able to give JM advice on his relationship with Xhex. Together, they faced the unresolved pain of Wellsie’s loss, and those moments affected me deeply. Their relationship is so important to this series, so I’m glad Ward came through in this manner.<br /><br /><b>Xhex and John Matthew</b><br />I was kind of frustrated with the issues in their relationship. They had been through so much, I wanted them to have smooth sailing. Regardless of my discomfort with their relationship troubles in this book, I have to say it made sense. JM had to learn to deal with his issues with his mate going out in the field and risking her life, and how that affected his bonded male emotions. I like that he did get past those issues and respect the fact that the female he’d fallen in love with wasn’t the stay at home type. She was a warrior in her own right (actually for many years before JM). That was why he loved her, because she was a tough, strong, independent woman. Who was he force her to turn her back on that? From Xhex’s standpoint, I don’t think she was being unreasonable. She had the right to be herself, even if she was JM’s mate. And it was annoying how the Brothers and even Rehv weren’t taking her seriously because JM wasn’t dealing well with the idea of her being in danger. I felt bad for her, because she really does love JM, and wants to be with him, but doesn’t want to deny who she is, and she’s been through too much to let go of her sense of identity just because she was in love. I could also understand JM’s fears, especially seeing how Tohr losing Wellsie destroyed him. He didn’t want to go through that by losing Xhex, because she is his life. I’m glad that they were able to get past this. Since they are my favorite couple in this series, I loved seeing a lot more of them, even if there were some troubled times in their relationship. <br /><br /><b>Band of Bastards</b><br />I wasn’t sure how things would go with the new storyline of the BoB. I have to say it was very interesting. I don’t view them as villains. I think that things will turn around for them to be allies with the Brotherhood, but it will be hard going. Xcor is a right b*stard, but he has grown on me. I hurt for him. I hope that he does find a female who finds him worthy, and hopefully that will be Layla. We’ll see. I was glad to get to know the other BoB, who now have names! Throe is still my favorite. He reminds me of Phury, in that he is a courtly male. That ain’t a bad thing at all, since I love me some Phury.<br /><br /><b>Qhuinn and Blay</b><br />Honestly, Qhuinn has gotten on my nerves a time or two, but overall he is a worthy male and I do believe that. In this book, I really liked him. He has matured beautifully. I felt bad for him that he had to see Blay with Saxton, but in some way, the eating his heart out has been good for him. I think now he will fight for what he could have with Blay, and I’m looking forward to that.<br /><br /><b>Lassiter</b><br />He cracks me up! I want to see more of him. I liked how he was a huge influence in getting Tohr and Autumn together and in helping them get past their issues. I want to see what this guy will be up to in the future, so I’m glad he’s sticking around.<br /><br /><b>Assail</b><br />I have a feeling I will like this character. More please!<br /><br /><b>Where is Murhder???? I need some Murhder!</b><br /><br /><b>Now…..If there was one thing I hated about this book…..</b><br />Why did Layla and Qhuinn have to sex because she went into her needing? It just felt all kinds of wrong to me. I am really unhappy about this outcome. If Qhuinn is going to be with Blay and Layla might end up with Xcor, what is the point of them having a child together? I just don’t see the blended family scenario working well in this series. I could be wrong. Maybe the WARDen will work it out. As for now, I am very unhappy about this! Sob! (Danielle admits that she thought about this all night‼)<br /><br /><b>Overall Thoughts</b><br />Unlike some fans (and former fans) of the series, I wasn’t worried that this book would suck. I knew I’d enjoy it because I truly love JR Ward’s writing. I feel that she truly wanted to give Tohr a good story, and the end results show it. I’m sure it was a hard book to write, with many emotional struggles for Ms. Ward in the process of putting it on paper. Even though I don’t always like some twists in the stories, the whole package works for me. <br /><br />This book touched me in so many ways. It had me laughing outrageously. It had me so sad that I couldn’t even cry. It made me happy. It was smoking hot as far as the plentiful love scenes, but it was also romantic. I felt she had given me resolution on some issues that were hanging out there in the air for me. I loved seeing some of my favorite characters who don’t get enough page time, like,….Phury. Too bad I didn’t get to see much of Cormia or Mary. I ain’t gonna lie, I would love more Rehv, but at least he was around in this book. It was great seeing Marissa again. I always feel great when I get to revisit my favorites, but part of me wants more! Heck, I think Ward tries. If she had pages of each of the characters, these books would be 1000 pages long, so I am not hating on her about it. I loved seeing all the Brothers stand up in support of Tohr in his difficult time. That was so necessary to this book. It warmed my heart big time. <br /><br />So, for this reader, the magic is still there. I am afraid of the book slump I see coming since I have finished this latest BDB book, and the countdown begins for the next book. Next year. I can make it! I know I can!<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4660317309833471312" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_607553402" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/607553402" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/607553402?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer607553402" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8289882843558922455"><b> 5 BDB Obsessed Stars! </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/a0e9ec60-13fa-46b4-aa0d-f779038cf723_zps113da89f.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833957._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo a0e9ec60-13fa-46b4-aa0d-f779038cf723_zps113da89f.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“God, I miss you,” he said in a voice that cracked. “Every night. Every day…”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br/>Even though Tohr’s shellan has been gone for a while, it still hasn’t gotten any easier for the brother. He is heartbroken, devastated, all he can do is fight the lessers, fight to avenge his shellans death. That’s all he has the strength for. <br/><br/>We meet No’One in book 8 (JM and Xhex’s book) She is Xhex’s mahmen, and she has been staying on this side to try to form a connection with h</span>
  <span id="freeText8289882843558922455" style="display:none"><b> 5 BDB Obsessed Stars! </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/a0e9ec60-13fa-46b4-aa0d-f779038cf723_zps113da89f.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420405i/833957._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo a0e9ec60-13fa-46b4-aa0d-f779038cf723_zps113da89f.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“God, I miss you,” he said in a voice that cracked. “Every night. Every day…”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Even though Tohr’s shellan has been gone for a while, it still hasn’t gotten any easier for the brother. He is heartbroken, devastated, all he can do is fight the lessers, fight to avenge his shellans death. That’s all he has the strength for. <br><br>We meet No’One in book 8 (JM and Xhex’s book) She is Xhex’s mahmen, and she has been staying on this side to try to form a connection with her daughter. Tohr and No’One have a past connection. They knew each other a long time ago, but Tohr is nothing like the male she knew back then. No’One hasn’t had an easy life either. After what happened to her long ago, she has dedicated her life to serving others on the other side. She hasn’t really had a life of her own. But that is starting to change. <br><br>Lassiter plays a much bigger part in this story. For his won reasons, he needs Tohr to move on, he is on a mission to free Wellsie from the In Between, and he can’t do that until Tohr gets himself together. Seeing how Tohr and No’One are together, Lassiter knows they would be great together. It starts out with a feeding. Tohr looks pitiful. He hasn’t been feeding well, and he needs to be strong. No’One volunteers to feed him. She completely understands that he is still not over Wellsie, and she is okay with that. Because of her past, she is not looking for a male. She tells Tohr it’s alright. It makes him feel a bit better. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Your shellan is welcome here.</blockquote>
</b><br>Tohr and No’One develop a relationship over time. Even though No’One never inteneds to, she starts to fall for Tohr. The feelings Tohr is having for No’One scare him. He shouldn’t be feeling this way. Not for anyone except Wellsie. It is devastating watching him try to move past all this. I love how Tohr renames No’One. She becomes Autumn. <br><b>
  <blockquote>To be named was to be claimed, and it made her feel... reborn.</blockquote>
</b> Autumn has trouble with her feelings for Tohr. She doesn't want him to know she loves him- she knows how he still feels about his shellan. Certain scenes between these two were so hard to read... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[During Autumn’s needing... so heartbreaking! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. But sometimes, you have to be able to forgive and move on. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/a31b5c5c-e2e4-4a19-b9d1-523219c57a1a_zps53e546c7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420406i/833958._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo a31b5c5c-e2e4-4a19-b9d1-523219c57a1a_zps53e546c7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is so much going on in this book with other characters as well. A lot of John Matthew and Xhex. Their relationship isn’t easy either. I was happy they were able to work it out. I was especially glad seeing JM and Tohr build their relationship back up. This was an emotional one for sure. The ending was beautiful! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/4f091747-a940-4445-a8f6-2f97fd96b5fc_zps47006382.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420406i/833959.jpg" alt=" photo 4f091747-a940-4445-a8f6-2f97fd96b5fc_zps47006382.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>On top of all the sad and heartbreaking, there was a lot of funny too...<br><br><i>“And if that bastard’s innocent,” Rhage spoke up, “I’m the fucking Easter bunny.” <br>“Oh, good,” someone quipped. “I’m calling you Hop-along Hollywood from now on.” <br>“Beasty Bo Peep,” somebody else threw out. <br>“We could put you in a Cadbury ad and finally make some money—” <br>“People,” Rhage barked, “the point is that he is not innocent and I’m not the Easter bunny—” <br>“Where’s your basket?” <br>“Can I play with your eggs?” <br>“Hop it out, big guy—” <br>“Will you guys fuck off ? Seriously!”</i><br><br>  And Lassiter is always good for a laugh too... I love his addiction to reality tv!<br><br><i>“You motherfucker! I knew you were the father!” Tohr fought the urge to slap some sense into the son of a bitch. His Wesslie’s future was at stake, and this dumb-ass was worried about Maury’s paternity tests? “Are you kidding me?” “No, I’m damn serious. Bastard has three kids by three different sisters- what kind of man is that?</i><br><br><br><br>Now, what I’ve been waiting for....<br>So, besides’s my Vishous- Qhuinn is my next favorite male in this series. I am SO STOKED for Qhuinn and Blay’s book I can’t even stand it! And what a perfect way Ward set up their story... I feel like every book it builds. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/ff4f8e69-33cc-49fa-afc1-109e42105fce_zps1d200ce8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420406i/833960.jpg" alt=" photo ff4f8e69-33cc-49fa-afc1-109e42105fce_zps1d200ce8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’m really curious to see if <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The Chosen Layla is pregnant, and if so, how that will effect Blay and Qhuinn’s relationship <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Either way, I just know this book will be amazing!!!<br><br><br>Now something I made just for fun- my casting of The Brotherhood:<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/d48ecbd0-aefa-4bdc-a8e0-56898844fd31_zps95bcb65a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794013i/585989._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo d48ecbd0-aefa-4bdc-a8e0-56898844fd31_zps95bcb65a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’ve said it once, I’ve said it a dozen times- If you haven’t read this series, YOU ARE SERIOUSLY MISSING OUT!!!!! It has quickly become one of my favorite series! <br><br>Now, I will wait patiently for my BDB girls Lisa Jayne &amp; Anna to catch up with me so we can EPICLY buddy read book 11 together :D </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
