<div id="review_186177343" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/186177343" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/186177343?book_show_action=true">Jul 18, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=angels-nephilim-and-demons">angels-nephilim-and-demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=multiple-pov">multiple-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=male-pov">male-pov</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=romantica-or-erotica">romantica-or-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=made-me-laugh">made-me-laugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=super-cheese">super-cheese</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer186177343" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16775688448999662854"><u>***Second Read November 2014***</u> As promised, I'm not re-reviewing all of the books because that seems like far too much work for what's meant to be a lazy and enjoyable series re-read. However, this book needed me to expand on some thoughts. There are series spoilers up through book 10, so please don't read this review if you aren't looking to be spoiled.<br/><br/>Why did I decide to add an additional note to this book in particular? Well, the reason is this : I'm doing it for the disgruntled BDB fans. Yo</span>
  <span id="freeText16775688448999662854" style="display:none"><u>***Second Read November 2014***</u> As promised, I'm not re-reviewing all of the books because that seems like far too much work for what's meant to be a lazy and enjoyable series re-read. However, this book needed me to expand on some thoughts. There are series spoilers up through book 10, so please don't read this review if you aren't looking to be spoiled.<br /><br />Why did I decide to add an additional note to this book in particular? Well, the reason is this : I'm doing it for the disgruntled BDB fans. You know who you are. You're the ones who are not thrilled with the series direction, or feel like the series is getting milked to death beyond where it needed to go. <br /><br />I understand. I really do. Trust me. I've been in a few discussions with people, offering up some of the same concerns. <br /><br />Yet, something clicked for me while doing this re-read. The series hasn't really changed in the way that people might think. Yes, there are tons of extra character (side) stories that weren't there in the original books - BUT when you really think about it, the space that's being taken up for Xcor, Assail, the Shades, etc. etc. etc. was, in fact, space that was occupied in the past by all of the lesser and Omega crap that a lot of us wanted to skim. At least, this way, the filler material actually has more interest and merit. <br /><br />The main character love stories might seem to be pushed out in favor of the side stories, but are they really? I've noticed on my re-read that no, this might not be the case. The books are just a little bit longer than they were before, so the extra pages are being used on side stories, which makes the main love story seem shorter, even though it really isn't. <br /><br />If you look at it from that perspective, the series has gotten better, not worse. There's less filler on the lesser front, and more new characters to love. Going back and reading Xcor's battle for supremacy made me fall in love with him all over again. He is truly the "beast" in the <i>Beauty and the Beast</i> story. <br /><br />Some of my complaints with <i>Lover Reborn</i> from my first read faded this time around. One of my biggest issues was feeling like Autumn and Tohr needed more of a spark - that it sucked not having him bond with Autumn in the way that he did with Wellsie - almost as if he would never love her the same. <br /><br />But I didn't get that this time. In fact, I noticed things about their relationship that I didn't notice at all on my first read. I remember feeling sort of cold to their relationship before, and this time, I had tears in my eyes when I read : <i>he'd never felt closer to anyone. Even his Wellsie.</i> <br /><br />HOW did I miss that before? Before, it almost seemed like Tohr and Autumn had this "consolation prize" relationship going on. This time, I saw them slowly fall in love into something deeper than a physical attraction (which I think I'd been looking for the first time around, which is why I was missing the MINE bonding shit). <br /><br />Oh, and there was a mention (sorry, I didn't highlight it for reference) of Tohr throwing out a male scent at some point. Maybe it was just a scent of arousal and not a bonding scent, but when I read it this time, it did strike me as a possessive scent. So even if it wasn't a "bonding" scent, he did/does have the capability to WANT to protect and coddle his female. <br /><br />And the scene where he fed her was beautiful. I feel like an idiot for really not seeing these things the first time around.<br /><br />So there we have it. I would encourage those who have grown weary of the series to consider doing a re-read. It's really made me appreciate the books even more this time around. All of the cheesy and annoying things that I've never liked about the series have somehow become amusing and nostalgic in a way because it is like revisiting an old friend - when you miss someone, you start to realize that the bothersome things aren't worth worrying about. <br /><br /><u>***Original Review March 2012***</u> <b>3.5 stars.</b> I didn't realize how much I'd longed for Ward's guilty-pleasure goodness until I picked up <i>Lover Reborn</i>. It was like taking a shot of adrenaline to my reading mojo. Thank goodness everyone knows these books have a HEA for the main characters (that's happily ever after for those not familiar with the term), so I won't be spoiling anything by putting (for the first time ever!) the last sentence of a book into my review : <i>
  <b>On that note, he kissed his female...and bit into his Big Mac.</b>
</i> YES. I missed my boys.<br /><br />I am one of the rare few who appreciates the latter books more than the former ones in this series. Even though Rhage and Z (books 2 and 3) will continue to remain some of my favorite "love stories," I am much more content with the transition of the series from straight PNR into a PNR/UF hybrid. One of the best features of this expanding world is how the lives of all of the Brotherhood have become intertwined. They live together, fight together, and share their struggles with one another. BDB now has more to offer because of its expanding to become something other than just a set of basic alpha-male love stories. It's too bad that those who were put off by the extreme cheesy testosterone of the first installment (probably the weakest in the series outside of Phury's book) never got to see the series hit a good stride.<br /><br />Did I say I missed my boys already? I did? Well, here's some more reasons why :<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"I'll teach the fucker to read," V muttered. "By cramming the Library of Congress up his ass."<br /><br />"Scotch? Gin? Bourbon?" the angel asked. "I'm having an Orgasm."<br />Tohr rubbed his face. "Can you never say that word around me when you're buck-ass nekkid?"<br />That set off a round of, "Orgaaaaaasmmmm, orgaaaaaaasmmm," to the tune of Beethoven's Fifth.<br /><br />"Aha!" Lassiter pointed at the boob tube. "You motherfucker! I knew you were the father!"<br />Tohr fought the urge to slap some sense into the son of a bitch. His future was at stake, and this dumb-ass was worried about Maury's paternity tests? "Are you kidding me?"<br />"No, I'm damn serious. Bastard has three kids by three sisters - what kind of a man is that?"</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Mild spoilers ahead for those who haven't read the book yet. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>High Points :</u>
</b><br /><br />1. Lassiter - snarky angel who watches Maury = good stuff<br />2. Offbeat humor - one of Ward's strengths as a writer<br />3. Layla/Xcor/Throe - picture me with a raised eyebrow<br />4. Tohr - not as much to say here but I'm glad he got a chance to heal<br /><br /><b>
  <u>Low Points :</u>
</b><br /><br />1. Pop culture references - there are still an over-abundance of these. I was starting to wonder if Ward was getting sponsored by all the brands, music, and items she mentioned. This is the stuff that dates the books. I'm letting Maury slide though because that was too perfect.<br />2. Tohr and No'One/Autumn's reunion. It was pretty yawn worthy. I'm a bit annoyed that <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he couldn't have had his MINE moment with her. I guess it's not the same when there's no bonding scent? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />3. John and Xhex - their drama dragged on for far too long.<br />4. Sexy time - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[when it was good, it was good. When I thought it was needed, it wasn't happening. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16775688448999662854" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Somethings I didnt always understand, or like but I appreciated the action-packed and emotional roller-coaster ride I escaped to for a few hours. She always cements with each new novel the extent of her writing prowess and as My fav writer.<br><br><i>The Main characters main me cry.....and that is all im going to comment on those two before i start weeping again.</i> This hot pic reminds me of them<a href="http://s754.photobucket.com/albums/xx188/earthzone/?action=view&amp;current=296498_106316919480633_100003069762235_51448_871449619_n.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380348247i/702499._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Now the other characters like Xcor <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[.....ammmm he tried to kill my Wrath...that is a huge no no <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> his attachment to someone I would not have ever dreamed would be possible or entered the scope of my imagination,but i have hope the Warden knows what she is about and the direction each character guides her. <b><br><br>oh and i absolutely I LOVE LASSITER. point, black period!!!!</b> just thought i'll put that in as well lol.<br><br>John and Xhex relationship had me on eggshells...but their continual make-up sex was HOTT!!!! Following pic reminds me of them <a href="http://s754.photobucket.com/albums/xx188/earthzone/?action=view&amp;current=536197_194999203945737_100003069762235_300498_1103656012_n.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380348247i/702500._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh and Warden introduced Assail and more names to the Band of Brothers who will hopefully be explained in future books. And that bit about Layla <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b> im tearing out my hair whyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyyy did it had to be my Qhuinn who deflowered her ahhhhhhhhhh</b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>I WILL FOREVER DESPISE NO HATE WHAT THE WARDEN DID THERE, still boggles my mind especially with what happens to my love peas possible future in the end <br><br><b>OK for the pièce de résistance; the last part with Blay and Qhuinn was freaking fantastic he quote</b><br><a href="http://s754.photobucket.com/albums/xx188/earthzone/?action=view&amp;current=s-ABERCROMBIE-AND-FITCH-GAY-ADS-large.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380348247i/702501.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><i>No one got forever. And it was a fucking crime to waste what you were given.<br>Enough, Qhuinn thought. Enough with the excuses, and the avoidance, and the trying to be someone, anyone else.<br>Even if he got shanked, even if his precious little ego and his dumb-ass little heart got shattered into a million pieces, it was time to stop the bullshit.<br>It was time to be a male.<br>As Blay started to straighten, like a message had been received, Qhuinn thought, That’s right, buddy.</i><br>Our future has come. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> unquote.<br><br>OMGGGGGG *freak out mode* Unfortunately im hyperventilating <br>and this will have to be the end of my review...Next Book CANT WAIT!!!<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_2030245414" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2030245414" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2030245414?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Vamps lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=paranormal-sci-fi-fantasy">paranormal-sci-fi-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2030245414" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7578824202398885118"><b>Genre: </b> Paranormal Romance<br/><b>Type: </b>Book 10 of Black Dagger Brotherhood series<br/><b>POV: </b>Third Person<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498005483i/23079146.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When Tohrment lost his shellan Wellsie, he lost part of himself too. Once a feared and respected leader of the Black Dagger Brotherhood, what left of him was just a shell of the male he used to be. What he didn't realize was as he suffered in living, so did she in the afterlife. He needed to move on to ease both of their suffering.<br/><br/>No'One knew suffering first hand. With a tragic past, she carried h</span>
  <span id="freeText7578824202398885118" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b> Paranormal Romance<br><b>Type: </b>Book 10 of Black Dagger Brotherhood series<br><b>POV: </b>Third Person<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498005483i/23079146.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When Tohrment lost his shellan Wellsie, he lost part of himself too. Once a feared and respected leader of the Black Dagger Brotherhood, what left of him was just a shell of the male he used to be. What he didn't realize was as he suffered in living, so did she in the afterlife. He needed to move on to ease both of their suffering.<br><br>No'One knew suffering first hand. With a tragic past, she carried her burden quietly, barely living the life bestowed upon her. She wanted to help Tohr find peace, but she had her own demons that needed exorcising.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>"You will always have my sympathy for everything you’ve been through, but I’ve got my own shit to deal with.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Throughout the series, Tohr has been moping and acting selfishly. While I understand his grief, it was time for him to man up. It took him a long time to "get it" and along his journey of acceptance, he wasn't exactly my favorite person lol!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>“I have no need or desire to take her place. And I accept you just as you are, in any fashion you choose to come to me. Or not, if that is the way it must be.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>No'One was probably the most passive character I've ever read. Her quiet gentleness not only stemmed from her upbringing, but also the result of her past. Her self esteem issue made me wanted to shake her at times.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>The truth was, she was calling something out of him, some kind of emotion, and those feelings were starting to turn gears inside of him that were rusted and cranky from lack of use. It terrified him. She terrified him.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>As tragic as it sounds with their own individual issues, I think both of them really were perfect for each other. Only someone who's been in the same hell would understand what it takes to get out of it. So even though both of them could be frustrating, I did enjoy the deeper part of the story.<br><br>I also like all the secondary stories. I hated Xcor when he was first introduced in the series, but he showed a different side of him in this book and I'm curious on how he'll evolve.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1498005484i/23079147.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lover Reborn is a story of two people learning to accept their past and help each other to move on. I'm looking forward to the next book especially that it's of one of my favorite character.<br><br><br><b>Standalone Books in the series:</b><br><i>Must be read in order</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/42899.Dark_Lover__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___1_" title="Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1429676285s/42899.jpg" alt="Dark Lover (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #1) by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/35729.Lover_Eternal__Black_Dagger_Brotherhood___2_" title="Lover Eternal (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #2) by J.R. Ward" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1300845974s/35729.jpg" alt="Lover Eternal (Black Dagger Brotherhood, #2) by J.R. Ward" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300337113" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15009637529733769701"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>To be named was to be claimed, and it made her feel … reborn.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><i>Lover Reborn</i> is the 10th book of the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> series. It is the story of Tohr and No'One (a.k.a. Autumn), and as usual, there are many other storylines.<br/><br/><b>Tohr and Autumn</b><br/><i>Lover Reborn</i> raises many questions and debates: why Wellsie wasn’t saved, like Jane and Mary? Is it too soon for Tohr to move on? Does No’One deserve a HEA? Is their love real, or is No’One only a substitute for Wellsie?<br/><br/>I was disappointed in To</span>
  <span id="freeText15009637529733769701" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>To be named was to be claimed, and it made her feel … reborn.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><i>Lover Reborn</i> is the 10th book of the <i>Black Dagger Brotherhood</i> series. It is the story of Tohr and No'One (a.k.a. Autumn), and as usual, there are many other storylines.<br /><br /><b>Tohr and Autumn</b><br /><i>Lover Reborn</i> raises many questions and debates: why Wellsie wasn’t saved, like Jane and Mary? Is it too soon for Tohr to move on? Does No’One deserve a HEA? Is their love real, or is No’One only a substitute for Wellsie?<br /><br />I was disappointed in Tohr’s “development”, and I think No’One is the least impressive “heroine” and their “love story” is the least satisfying in the BDB series. Sorry for the quotations marks but you get my point, right?<br /><br />I liked their backstory which was revealed in <i>Lover Unleashed.</i> It could have been a great base for the romance, but the execution was superficial, hasty, and utterly unsatisfying.<br /><br /><b>Lassiter</b><br />I always loved him, but now… I have no words. I hope he'll have his own story.<br /><br /><b>John and Xhex</b><br />Xhex and John’s marriage crisis started interesting, and I sympathized with both of them, for different reasons. Sadly, it became flat in the middle of the story, and ended in a predictable way. But I still love them together, and like the insights of the marriage of Vishous and Jane in <i>Lover Unleashed</i>, this secondary storyline was also refreshing.<br /><br /><b>Xcor and the Band of Bastards</b><br />Despite their <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[assassination attempt against the king, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I can’t take the B.o.B. seriously. But the characters are intriguing.<br /><br />First Xcor seemed to be only a power-greedy, not too smart maniac with a ridiculously absurd aim. Even his soldiers realized that “with a mind like his and plans such as he had, that was not a good combination.” Of course, these traits are still his, and just because he has an abusive past, it doesn't make him likeable. But slowly it is revealed that he has compassion, principles, and he is capable of regret. So he has values, but also very bad political senses. I still don’t like him, but his character is definitely promising.<br /><br /><b>Qhuinn and Blay</b><br />Qhuinn is totally consumed by his feelings for Blay, by the anguish of their situation and his future in general. He still stagnates in the same emotional state, as he did in the previous book, <i>Lover Unleashed</i>. To my utter disappointment, I can’t see any development. He is still disillusioned, still jealous, still lonely, still in anguish, still feeling himself to be an outcast. He doesn’t communicate, not with Blay, and not with anyone else.<br /><br />In spite of their book being the next one in the series, I felt Qhuinn and Blay’s storyline neglected in this installment. Of course their story has been building up since <i>Lover Enshrined</i>, so actually I’m complaining because I didn’t get enough of them in <i>Lover Reborn</i>. Qhuinn’s heroic (or insanely brave) act made me very proud of him, and I really looking forward to their book.<br /><br /><b>Qhuinn and Layla</b><br />Their hasty decision is questionable. We’ll see…<br /><br /><b>Xcor and Layla</b><br />What the author doesn’t manage to achieve with the Band of Bastards, she does with the attraction between Layla and Xcor. This thing between Layla and Xcor would make a nice conflict. I would really love to see it!<br /><br /><b>Assail</b><br />Seriously? Who’s that guy? And why should I care about him?<br /><br /><b>I missed very much the King’s viewpoint.</b> Considering the political situation they are in, not presenting Wrath’s thoughts is a big defect of the novel. <br /><br /><b>All in all.</b> Lover Reborn is one of the weakest (or let's be honest, actually the weakest) book of the series. And now, for the second read, and also having read the following two books, I can see that this book was where the series started to go downhill. But it is an amazing and outstanding series up to this installment, and it will be always one of my favorite PNR series.<br /><br /><a href="http://exinasreadings.tumblr.com/tagged/Lover-Reborn" rel="nofollow noopener">My favorite quotes.</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="15009637529733769701" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11194947807023191762"><b>5 hand-to-my-heart-and-tears-falling ~ STARS !!!!</b> I loved this book !!!<br/><br/>My Tohr❤❤<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852706._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>I will love one and only one female for the rest of my life. No matter what I do, who I'm with, or how things appear, you can take that shit to the bank, son. We clear?"</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Tohr broke my heart throughout this whole book. ( except for the one part where he took a stupid pill and ripped my heart out ....)<br/>The love of his life Wellsie had been killed earlier in the series. He was as devastated as if it happened just yest</span>
  <span id="freeText11194947807023191762" style="display:none"><b>5 hand-to-my-heart-and-tears-falling ~ STARS !!!!</b> I loved this book !!!<br><br>My Tohr❤❤<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852706._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>I will love one and only one female for the rest of my life. No matter what I do, who I'm with, or how things appear, you can take that shit to the bank, son. We clear?"</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Tohr broke my heart throughout this whole book. ( except for the one part where he took a stupid pill and ripped my heart out ....)<br>The love of his life Wellsie had been killed earlier in the series. He was as devastated as if it happened just yesterday. He had nothing to live for except to avenge his shellans death. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852707._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wellsie.......is stuck in the "In Between". For her to rest in peace in the Fade....Tohrment must finally let her go......along with Lassiter's help....Wellsie can finally be at eternal rest.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852708._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❤<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852709._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>❤<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794658i/595235.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You with the <b>sad eyes </b> come to Mama ~ I will help you heal your broken heart ! You will love again ❤<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852710._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>Just so that you and I are utterly clear with each other, I have no interest in any male. I am sexually repulsed by your kind, and that includes yourself.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Tohrment and No'One have crossed paths before. Many, many years ago. <br><br>I really loved No'One/Autumns character. She was extremely patient, so kind, so compassionate, and my heart bled for her troubled past. She had a fall from grace that made her feel like lesser of a person. I was committed to her happily-ever-after too !!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"I don't want to hurt you." he said<br>"You won't. I know you are still in love with your mate, and I do not blame you. What you had with her was a once-in-a-lifetime love."<br>"What about you?"<br>"I have no need or desire to take her place. And I accept you as you are, in any fashion you choose to come to me. Or not, if that is the way it must be. I am happy to simply have time with you. That is enough-and more that I could ever have expected out of my fate."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Such a beautiful, gripping story...I honestly was blown away...once again. I closed this book and thought about how precious life is. The circle of life really is amazing. Every character that I loved from previous books, in this book, really stepped up to the plate and wow...just blew me away. <br><br><b>Lassiter</b>.....<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852711.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>My names's Lassiter, and I'll tell you all you need to know about me. I'm an angel first, and a sinner second, and I'm not here for long. I'll never hurt you, but I'm prepared to make you pretty goddamn uncomfortable if I have to, to get my job done."</blockquote><br><br>I've got my eyes on you Angel ❤ thank you for taking one for the TEAM !<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852712.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Especially after this tidbit of yummilicious information:<br><blockquote>"Wow," she breathed.<br>"I know, right? Hung like a horse."<br>"If you're really nice--and you live through this--I'll promise not to tell V."<br>"About my size."</blockquote>......alrightyyyyy then ! So moving on ..... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852713.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Qhuinn❤did some EPIC EPIC shit in this book !!! I can't wait for his book !!! Up next with Lisa Jayne and Christy ....are you ready?? True true true</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426651i/852714.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>❤❤❤</span>

<div id="review_169555804" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/169555804" />
    <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583236251p2/3575839.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/169555804?book_show_action=true">May 19, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780749955700" href="/book/show/11540581-lover-reborn">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=va-va-voom-vampires">va-va-voom-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-i-wanna-hug">hero-i-wanna-hug</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-j-r-ward">author-j-r-ward</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=fugly-cover">fugly-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=why-is-the-us-cover-always-better">why-is-the-us-cover-always-better</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer169555804" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14633184853874774506">Woohoo! release day at last and I can put my review up!<br/>Review also on: <a href='http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/2012/03/review-lover-reborn-by-jr-ward.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Under the Covers</a><br/><br/>We are now on the tenth Black Dagger Brotherhood book and I still love this series as much as I did when I started Dark Lover, for me this series never gets old. When I first started reading though I never though Tohrment would need a book of his own, he already had his shellan, Wellsie, but shit happens and Tohr is now drowning in his own grief, which is not only killing himself, but is preventing Wellsie and</span>
  <span id="freeText14633184853874774506" style="display:none">Woohoo! release day at last and I can put my review up!<br />Review also on: <a href="http://underthecoversbookblog.blogspot.co.uk/2012/03/review-lover-reborn-by-jr-ward.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Under the Covers</a><br /><br />We are now on the tenth Black Dagger Brotherhood book and I still love this series as much as I did when I started Dark Lover, for me this series never gets old. When I first started reading though I never though Tohrment would need a book of his own, he already had his shellan, Wellsie, but shit happens and Tohr is now drowning in his own grief, which is not only killing himself, but is preventing Wellsie and his son from going to the Fade. Which, brings us to Lassiter's mission: Get Tohr over Wellsie so she can move on to the Fade. Could No'One be the answer?<br /><br />It was such a tradegy when Wellsie died, I remember reading it, dreading Tohr's reaction when he found out, then sobbing like a girl when he did. So when I received Lover Reborn through the post I was both excited to see what would happen, how Tohr and No'One would connect and also anxious I mean Tohr and Wellsie just fit so well together how could No'One possibly live up to that? After having read it, I still have mixed feelings, this romance is so different from the others, vastly more complicated, more mature and though I was very pleased in the end sometimes it was painful to read their progression. Mainly I think because I am not a huge fan of No'One she is like a vampire doormat, her placid and accepting nature annoyed the shit out of me, although I know that is she had been any more aggressive the romance wouldn't have happened in the first place. So you see; mixed feelings.<br /><br />But, although the couple wasn't my favourite what I adored about this book was the Band of Bastards. Love. Them. They have their very own Brotherhood which is both darker and more violent then the original and they are definietly stepping up their game in their bid to put Xcor on the throne. The face off between B.o.B and the Brotherhood is going to be explosive and even more tense because I like characters from both sides, one of the reasons I am jonesing for the next book is so I can see more of them. Also...Love Triangle Alert involving Throe, Xcor and a certain unnamed female....<br /><br />Qhuinn and Blay Update. Man people are going to be pissed at some of the developments in this book, but how the last chapter ended with those two...we need the Qhuay book. NOW.<br /><br />I loved this book, the romance wasn't particularly my favourite but there are so many other things to love about it and all I can't think about right now is getting my hands on the next book in the series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="14633184853874774506" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4q+c1I3WhVEFM2JWcTOsl2w2NSpQH10j0Lx+3uAoPYPYifUGNohMOaIY1jeGxqZIumnS4p6S00SLwjhvLWvPGQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }
